UPDATE `fo_curves` SET `fo_next_curve_id`=`id`+1 WHERE `fo_track_id`=2 AND `name` NOT LIKE "#7";
UPDATE `fo_curves` SET `fo_next_curve_id`=`id`-6 WHERE `fo_track_id`=2 AND `name` LIKE "#7";

UPDATE `fo_positions`
	SET `fo_curve_id` = (SELECT `id` FROM `fo_curves` WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `name` LIKE "#1")
	WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `order` > 33 AND `order` < 71 AND `order` NOT IN (35, 37, 69);
UPDATE `fo_positions`
	SET `fo_curve_id` = (SELECT `id` FROM `fo_curves` WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `name` LIKE "#2")
	WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `order` > 99 AND `order` < 121 AND `order` NOT IN (101);
UPDATE `fo_positions`
	SET `fo_curve_id` = (SELECT `id` FROM `fo_curves` WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `name` LIKE "#3")
	WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `order` > 167 AND `order` < 193 AND `order` NOT IN (191);

	WHERE `fo_track_id` = 2 AND `order` > 560 AND `order` < 621 AND `order` NOT IN (562, 564, 619);
